# OpenTrade 當前狀態

> ⚠️ **這是項目最動態的文件，每個 session 必讀必寫。**
> 任何 AI agent 開始工作前，必須先讀本檔取得最新進度。
> 任何 AI agent 結束 session 前，必須更新本檔。

---

`<label>`-wraps-input pattern — 早期 prototype 用 `<div role="button">` 結果 axe-core 雙報 nested-interactive + missing label，且 click + Enter 雙觸發；重構後完全靠瀏覽器原生 input behavior，0 axe violations + 無 JS 手寫鍵盤事件；(b) ApiClientError message 永不顯示給 user（per errorMessage.ts 設計），server side 'developer-only message' 只進 log — 跨 endpoint codes 全走 i18n；(g) M7.7 tests commit 1189 行 diff 超 rule 96 200 行但純測試 case 接受（rule 96 例外條款）。**rule 99 self-review**：本 session 所有改動皆照既有 patterns（DDD 4-layer / cva primitive / caller-supplied labels per rule 10 / next-intl 本地化 / next/link locale-aware navigation / Playwright stub + commit `86a48df` `docs(status): track phased broker defense rights and M7 plan refinement`**（28 insertions / 12 deletions = 40 行 diff）— 在 §中期 段 refine M7 plan 9 commits 詳述 + 新增 §被投訴方答辯權階段化實現追蹤 段 — STAGING.md S8 範圍 + 30-50 種子用戶量小 + 已比 WikiFX 公平）。**M7.1 commit `cedd5a7` `feat(db): add ReviewKind discriminator and complaint columns per ADR-0029`**（87 insertions = 87 行 diff，含 73 行 schema + 14 行 migration + 1 行 export）— `packages/db/prisma/schema.prisma` 加 `enum ReviewKind { REVIEW COMPLAINT }`（緊接 `Sentiment` enum 後）+ Review model 加 6 個 nullable complaint columns（`kind ReviewKind @default(REVIEW)` + `evidenceIpfsCid String?` + `verifiedAt DateTime?` + `verifiedByUserId String? @db.Uuid` + `respondsToReviewId String? @db.Uuid` 純 column 不 wire bidirectional relation 待 M10 商戶 broker response API 落地 + `adminNote String? @db.Text` 沿用 SbtVerificationRequest 既有 reject reason pattern）+ composite index `[tenantId, brokerId, kind, verifiedAt]` 給 M7.6a sentimentAggregate（WHERE kind=REVIEW）+ verifiedComplaintCount（WHERE kind=COMPLAINT AND verifiedAt IS NOT NULL）兩個 aggregate query 用；migration `20260526034736_add_review_kind_discriminator` SQL 乾淨（`CREATE TYPE` + `ALTER TABLE ADD COLUMN` 6 行 with `kind` 用 `NOT NULL DEFAULT 'REVIEW'` 是 Postgres 11+ fast-default 元數據改動不 rewrite table + `CREATE INDEX`，**無 UPDATE** 嚴守 rule 31 紅線）；`packages/db/src/index.ts` 加 `ReviewKind` re-export 保字母序。**M7.2 commit `39bf320` `feat(api): add complaint outbox event vocabulary with ack-only handlers`**（27 insertions / 3 deletions = 30 行 diff）— `apps/api/src/tasks/outbox-worker.ts` poll loop 加三個 explicit ack-only `else if` 分支（`complaint.submitted` / `complaint.verified` / `complaint.rejected`）沿用 M1.4 後續為 `verification.broker_added` 加的同 pattern，避免 `Unknown event type` warn noise；Phase 1 不上鏈 per ADR-0029 D7，handler 純 fall through 到 `processedAt` 更新；header docstring 同步把三個新 event type 列入 currently handles 段 + 為 `complaint.rejected` 特別注明 rule 00「reject != delete」worker MUST NOT 改 Review row。**M7.3a commit `968fc0f` `feat(api): bootstrap complaints domain types and Prisma repository`**（424 insertions = 424 行 diff，atomic-but-large 借 M5.1 + M6.0 + M6.2a 先例 — 三檔型態互依不能拆）— 新 `apps/api/src/domains/complaints/` 目錄 + 三檔：(a) `domain/ComplaintEntity.ts`（116 行）`SubmitComplaintInput` + `ComplaintRecord` + 派生 `ComplaintVerificationStatus`（`OPEN` / `VERIFIED` / `REJECTED` 三態，**從 **本 session 末發現 critical bug**：M6.3b Playwright run 與 user 的 `pnpm dev` 共用 `apps/web/.next/cache/webpack/` 導致 webpack 把 `NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL=http://127.0.0.1:4010` inline 進 bytecode + 寫進共用快取，user 的 `.next-e2e/types/**/*.ts` 給 typed routes + exclude `.next-e2e/{cache,server,static}` 避免 tsc 吃 build output；重跑 e2e 3/3 仍綠 + `.next/` 與 `.next-e2e/` 物理隔離。User 急救：`rm -rf apps/web/.next` 後 dev server refresh recompile 即恢復。**M6 收尾驗證點**：7 commits 全 lint-staged + prettier hooks pass + `pnpm --filter @opentrade/web typecheck` 綠（其他 workspace 在 M5 already 綠 未動）；新增 +72 unit/component tests（API 45 + UI 36 z.enum(['POSITIVE','NEUTRAL','NEGATIVE']).optional()` query param + WHERE 條件 spread；response item map 加 `sentiment: r.sentiment` cast；JSDoc 注明 sentiment 三值 selectivity 高，Postgres partial range scan 加 nullable enum + `fetchAdminReviews` 參數加 `sentiment?`；`ReviewsClient.tsx` 加 4-option sentiment filter dropdown（並排 status filter）+ 表格 column 換 `thRating → thSentiment` + cell 換新 `<SentimentCell>` helper（POSITIVE/NEUTRAL/NEGATIVE chip + null sentiment 顯示 `legacyRatingCaption` 不再 render 任何 star widget）；3 admin locale messages 加 `thSentiment/allSentiments/sentimentPositive/Neutral/Negative/legacyRatingCaption/legacyRatingCaptionTooltip` 7 keys（共 21 字串）。**M5.6 commit `ec0c07f`**（202 行 diff，含 3 個 console surface 改寫 + 6 locale block）— 完成 ADR-0028 D7 sweep，把 console 中尚存的 3 個五星 widget surface 統一改 sentiment chip + null-sentiment legacy caption：(a) `apps/console/src/app/[locale]/brokers/[slug]/page.tsx`（merchant detail server rule 22 storybook-as-companion 紅線）；(c) RatingSummary→SentimentDistribution 純 local function rename（單 callsite），沒檔名改、沒 import 重寫，rule 96 atomic 通過；(d) legacy null-sentiment caption pattern 跨 3 個 ADR-0027 author-original 落 locale）/ `contentHash=0xaf06e67a42abee23...`；on-chain receipt 確認 ReviewSubmitted event topic0 `0x1fa5b00888507bb5...` emit + worker log `"Review confirmed on-chain"` 完整匹配。**ADR-0021 + ADR-0022 + ADR-0025 + ADR-0027 整 stack 證實對全新 wallet 端到端可運作**。Phase 1 進度 96% → 99%，剩三條非 critical 收尾項：console Google UI 修復 / production DB 雙腳本 backfill / IPFS gateway charset proxy。**(12) ADR-0027 廢除 UGC 自動翻譯 + outbox SBT mint idempotency 守護 + Phase 1 E2E 部分驗證** — 接 user (a) Phase 1 ~93% handoff，本 session 同時推進 3 條軸線：**【軸線 1：環境健康度修復】**user 報「上一個 agent 改完有很多 error」，根因為前 session 裝 `opencc-js` 後 pnpm 重新 hash `.pnpm/` content store，但 next dev / api tsx watch 仍 cache 舊 module path，造成 `Module not found: viem/chains` 與 `ENOENT viem chains/index.js`；修復路徑：kill 全部 dev process、清 `apps/web/.next` + `apps/console/.next` (~1.1 GB)、`pnpm install --frozen-lockfile` 確認 lock 一致、重啟 dev。User 後確認「登入及 review 都沒有問題了」。**【軸線 2：outbox E2E partial verify + SBT mint idempotency 守護（commit 9df2336）】** user 在 zh-Hant 環境提交一筆 review「app不好用 / app不好用，經常死機，不推薦」，後續逐步驗證：DB 寫入正確 → outbox worker poll 到 `review.submitted` event → submitReview() on-chain → 收到 `ReviewSubmitted` event → Review.status PENDING→CONFIRMED + chainReviewId/txHash 填上 → Base Sepolia explorer txn `0x481ae26...` 上鏈 → Pinata IPFS payload (`bafkreid2hr...`) UTF-8 raw bytes 正確（瀏覽器看到的亂碼是 Pinata gateway HTTP response 缺 `charset=utf-8` header 的 cosmetic 問題，curl + Python decode 確認 raw bytes 是「app不好用」/「app不好用，經常死機，不推薦」）。多券商 E2E (i)(ii)(iv) 從 DB query 確認、(iii) 從 user `/verify` 截圖確認；同時診斷出 outbox worker `processSbtMintRequested` 對同 wallet 重複 mint 會被合約 `AlreadyMinted(address)` revert（selector `0x893cc576`），worker 會 retry 5 次才 terminal-fail，浪費 gas + 污染 log。Commit `9df2336` 在 `apps/api/src/tasks/outbox-worker.ts` 加 `balanceOf` ABI + idempotency guard：mint 前查 `ReviewerSBT.balanceOf(walletAddress)`，>0 → skip mint + log warn + 標 event processed；ADR-0025 多券商驗證 (broker A 後接 broker B) 自此不會再炸 worker。**【軸線 3：ADR-0027 廢除自動翻譯 + ADR-0023 superseded（4 atomic commits 86ecc95 + 8603252 + 003aa67 + aec13d8）】** user 觀察「用戶 review 目前在切換語言時，不會翻譯，但我認為是正確，因為是用戶語言，不用硬翻譯」，本 session 把這個觀察形式化：(d1) `docs(decisions,rules)` 寫 [ADR-0027](./decisions/0027-deprecate-ugc-translation.md) 8 個 D + 4 個 alternatives + 詳細 Consequences + 4-commit implementation plan，superseding ADR-0023；論點：(a) HK 金融用語（孖展、補倉、窩輪、結算）DeepL 易誤譯反失可信度，(b) 平台自動改寫 UGC 與「平台不介入內容」紅線在邊緣相觸，(c) GitHub / Reddit / Twitter / Glassdoor 業界 UGC 平台皆不自動翻譯，(d) 同源 CJK 跨地讀者基本可被動讀繁中，跨 locale 落差被 ADR-0023 高估；ADR-0023 status → Superseded + README index 同步 + rule 51 §UGC 翻譯段整段重寫（從 7-step DeepL flow 改 author-original + sourceLocale 寫入 + 嚴禁清單加 4 條紅線：不可 submit 自動譯 / 不可從 review_translations 服務 / 不可移除 dormant 設施 / 不可加新 provider env）。(d2) `feat(api)` 拆 SubmitReviewUseCase translationService ctor param + 刪 try-catch DeepL block；`ReviewEntity.SubmitReviewInput` 加 required `sourceLocale: 'zh-Hant' | 'zh-Hans' | 'en'`；`PrismaReviewRepository.create` 寫入 sourceLocale；`ReviewRecord` 暴露 nullable column；`POST /v1/reviews` zod body 加 optional sourceLocale + 新 `resolveSourceLocale()` helper 三層 priority（body explicit → exact Accept-Language match → zh-Hant 預設）；`GET /broker/:slug` 永遠回原文不 join `review_translations`、加 `sourceLocale` 進 response、刪 `isTranslated/originalTitle/originalBody`（grep 確認無前端 consumer）；`DeepLTranslationService` 加 class-level `@deprecated` JSDoc 指 ADR-0027；`env.ts` `DEEPL_API_KEY` JSDoc 從 ADR-0023 改 ADR-0027 @deprecated；DI wiring 停止 instantiate translationService。Typecheck + lint clean (剩 `brokers/routes.ts` 1 個 pre-existing warning)。(d3) `feat(web)` `apps/web/src/lib/api/client.ts` `ReviewItem` 加 `sourceLocale` nullable + `SubmitReviewInput` 加 required；`BrokerDetailTabs.tsx` SubmitReviewCta 加 `useLocale()` + 送 sourceLocale，ReviewsTab 上方加 `Info` icon + disclaimer，ReviewCard verified-broker badge container 並排加 sourceLocale neutral pill (white/5 background, suppress when null pre-D8-backfill)；`ReviewForm.tsx` 同步加 useLocale + sourceLocale；三語 messages 加 5 個 `brokerDetail.*` keys (reviewDisclaimer + sourceLocaleZhHant/zhHans/en + sourceLocaleTooltip)；繁中「繁體中文 / 簡體中文 / 英文」、簡中「繁体中文 / 简体中文 / 英文」、en「Traditional Chinese / Simplified Chinese / English」。Typecheck pass + lint baseline 完全不變（10 個 pre-existing errors 已 git stash 對比確認）。(d4) `feat(db)` 新 `packages/db/scripts/backfill-source-locale.ts` 實作 ADR-0027 D8 — Han-ratio (CJK Unified `[\u3400-\u4DBF\u4E00-\u9FFF]`) + OpenCC `t2s` 來回比對：< 30% Han → `en`、>= 30% Han 且 OpenCC output 不變 → `zh-Hans`、>= 30% Han 且 output 變了 → `zh-Hant`；reuse `backfill-zh-hans.ts` 的 mutable-WHERE + stall guard 模式（per ADR-0026 lesson）；wire `db:backfill:source-locale` script；dev DB 跑成功 — a2 review (繁中) → `zh-Hant`、5/22 seed review (英文) → `en`，手動 verify 兩 row 內容皆正確分類。Phase 1 進度 92% → 96%。**(11) ADR-0026 zh-Hans broker name strategy 6-commit 實作完成** — 把上一 session 拍板的方案 A 落地，6 個 atomic commit：(c1) `feat(db)` 加 `Broker.displayNameZhHans String?` 欄位（nullable 留 OpenCC 失敗 + admin override 出口）+ migration `20260524134053_add_broker_display_name_zh_hans` apply 到本機 DB；(c2) `feat(shared)` 把 `localizedBrokerName(b, locale)` helper 擴成三路 fallback（en → legalName / zh-Hans → displayNameZhHans / zh-Hant → displayName），`LocalizedNameInput` 加 `displayNameZhHans?: string | null` + 把 interface 改 type alias（lint fix），function 內加 `if (locale === 'zh-Hans')` 分支；(c3) `feat(db)` 裝 `opencc-js@1.3.1` + 新 `src/sfc/opencc.ts` lazy singleton converter（`t → cn` mapping per ADR-0026 D2）+ `sync-brokers.ts` 在每個 upsert 自動 `toSimplifiedChinese(legalNameZh)` + new script `scripts/backfill-zh-hans.ts`（batched fetch null rows, stall guard, idempotent on rerun，dev DB 全 3482 broker 一次性 backfill 完成）；(c4) `feat(api)` 把 `displayNameZhHans` ship 進 10 個 endpoint payload —— brokers list / detail / similarBrokers / admin/claims、admin users list / detail、admin reviews、auth me、verification-status、admin/verifications、reviews/broker/:slug top-level + author.verifiedBrokers —— 並升級 `apps/api/src/shared/brokerHydration.ts#BrokerNameMeta` 加 `readonly displayNameZhHans: string | null`（給 slug-keyed UserVerifiedBroker 用的 hydrate helper 已同步擴）；(c5) `feat(web,console)` 把 `displayNameZhHans` 展平進兩 app 的 `lib/api/client.ts` 全部 broker 引用 type + 10 個 component 中 hand-rolled props type（VerifyForm local Broker 型別、BrokerDirectory 局部 type + resolveBrokerName 加 zh-Hans 分支、BrokerDetailTabs similar brokers、settings/page、verify/page、brokers/page、admin UsersClient BrokerPills、admin rule 51 §模式 A 全面升 ship 三列（A1 helper 三路 fallback 改寫、A2 API contract 改 ship displayName+displayNameZhHans+legalName + 加禁止只回兩列的 ❌ 範例、A3 加「hand-rolled props 型別必須列三列」紅線、A4 加「zh-Hant/zh-Hans 不互當 [`2026-05-24-broker-name-i18n-and-zh-hans.md`](./conversations/2026-05-24-broker-name-i18n-and-zh-hans.md)。**(9) Broker name i18n hardening — 涵蓋全平台 + cursor rule 51 紅線** — 6 個 commit 應對 user-reported "前後台顯示券商的名字也要根據多語言顯示，這個已經很多次，要加到 cursor rules"。Audit subagent 找到 8 個顯示 raw slug + 6 個顯示 displayName-only（Chinese-only leak）的 surfaces。(9a) `feat(shared)` 把 `localizedBrokerName(b, locale)` lift 到 `packages/shared/src/i18n/brokerName.ts` 作為 canonical helper（pure function、`en → legalName ?? displayName ?? slug`、其他 → `displayName ?? legalName ?? slug`）。(9b) `feat(api)` 修 9 個 endpoints 一律 ship `UserVerifiedBroker` 這種 slug-keyed 表用，避免 N+1）。(9c) `feat(web)` 改 4 檔（client.ts types + VerifyForm + BrokerDetailTabs + settings/page.tsx）— 刪 inline localizedBrokerName 改用 shared helper、所有 當文案 / avatar initials 直接吃 displayName.charAt(0)）。**(8) ADR-0025 post-rollout fixes** — 2 個 follow-up commit 修兩個 user-reported 問題：(8a) `feat(db)`：寫 `20260524124500_backfill_user_verified_brokers` migration 把 ADR-0025 實作前 APPROVED 的 SbtVerificationRequest 全 backfill 到 `user_verified_brokers` 表（用 `verificationId` 為 join key + `ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING` 冪等，不 emit outbox event 避免假通知）— 解決 user 在 `/settings` 看到「尚未通過任何券商驗證」但 `/verify` 又被擋的 ledger drift bug；(8b) `feat(api,web)`：把 verify-broker 的 5 個 throw 加 machine-readable `details.reason`（`pending_exists` / `broker_already_verified` / `no_file` / `invalid_file_type` / `file_too_large`）、新增共用 helper `apps/web/src/lib/api/errorMessage.ts` `translateApiError(err, tErrors, fallbackText?)` 做 reason → code → fallback 兩層 i18n lookup（allow-listed Set 防 next-intl missing-key crash）、三語 messages 加 top-level `errors` namespace（9 個 ErrorCode + 5 個 reason）、`VerifyForm` 兩個 catch 改用 helper — 解決前端顯示 `You have already been verified for this broker` 等英文 raw message 的 i18n 漏洞。**(1)** `/verify` page status-driven views — 把「提交成功只顯示綠色 success card」升級為四態狀態機（loading / idle / pending / rejected / approved）。Pending card 採 Google reference 設計（amber Clock spinner + commitment hash + 提交時間 + 狀態 badge）。Rejected card 顯示 admin 駁回原因（紅框 readonly）+ 提交/駁回時間 + 「重新申請」button → 重設 form。Approved 顯示 alreadyVerified card。提交成功後自動 synthesise 一筆 PENDING 記錄即時切到 pending card。(2) Admin reject reason 必填 — API 拆 `approveActionSchema` / `rejectActionSchema`（reject `adminNote` min 5 max 500 chars，VALIDATION_ERROR on missing），console 加 nested `RejectReasonModal`（z-70）+ case modal data panel 顯示 `adminNote` 紅框 readonly。(3) Console admin verifications IPFS preview — 表格加 thumbnail 欄、case modal 兩欄式 layout（IPFS viewer 含 image zoom / PDF iframe / unknown fallback；data panel 顯示 broker / wallet / commitment / CID / adminNote）。`useEvidenceMime` hook 對 legacy 無 mime 紀錄走 HEAD probe Pinata gateway。`/verify` upload 加圖片即時 thumbnail（`URL.createObjectURL` + cleanup revoke）。(4) DB schema：`SbtVerificationRequest.evidenceMimeType String?` + 兩個 migrations（`add_user_credential_auth` baseline 修 schema drift + `add_verification_evidence_mime_type`）。(5) **ADR-0025 多券商驗證策略決策** — 採 B 漸進版（Phase 1 用 DB `UserVerifiedBroker` 表 + outbox hash chain；Phase 2 升 ReviewerSBT v2 鏈上化）。L 等級不靠驗證次數升、broker 數量不限、`(userId, brokerSlug)` 已 APPROVED 後不可重提。(6) **ADR-0025 Phase 1 實作完成** — 6 個 commit：DB 加 `user_verified_brokers` 表 + partial unique index `WHERE status='APPROVED'`；API approve flow 改 transaction（先查 prev commitment → insert UserVerifiedBroker → emit `verification.broker_added` outbox event with hash chain → 條件升 tier 只在 L1 → L2 第一次）+ `POST /verify-broker` 加 `(userId, brokerSlug)` APPROVED CONFLICT 防呆；`/verification-status` + `/admin/verifications` response 加 `verifiedBrokers` 陣列；`/verify` 加 `'adding'` viewMode + `BrokerCombobox.excludeSlugs` + `VerifyApprovedCard` broker list + `+N` overflow）。(7) **ADR-0025 verified broker 全平台覆蓋** — 4 個追加 commit：`/admin/users` API + Console（user list 加 `verifiedBrokers` pill 欄 + detail panel broker list，single Prisma include 避免 ### M0 + M1 + M2: 14-milestone 計畫前三階段（前 session 完成）

**M0 — 會議歸檔（2 commits）**

### Phase 1 MVP-A Block 1-3（前 session 完成）

Branch: `feature/phase-1-mvp-a`（first 4 commits + 1 handoff docs commit）

- [x] **Block 1: packages/config chain setup** — `chains.ts`（Base / Base Sepolia from viem, `getTargetChain()`, `SupportedChainId`）+ `contracts.ts`（`buildContractAddresses()` factory driven by env）+ `locales.ts`（`supportedLocales` / `defaultLocale` / `isSupportedLocale()`）+ viem 加入依賴。Subpath exports `@opentrade/config/{chains,contracts,locales}` 可用。
- [x] **Block 2b: Web3Providers** — `@privy-io/react-auth` + `@privy-io/wagmi` + `wagmi` + `viem` + `@tanstack/react-query` + `permissionless` 安裝到 apps/web。`Web3Providers.tsx`（PrivyProvider > SmartWalletsProvider > QueryClientProvider > WagmiProvider）嵌入 layout。`env.ts` 加 `NEXT_PUBLIC_PRIVY_APP_ID` + `NEXT_PUBLIC_CHAIN_ID`。`.env.example` 更新。
- [x] **Block 2c+2d: API identity domain + ES256 JWT + auth middleware** — identity domain DDD 四層（domain: `AuthenticatedUser` + `IUserRepository`；application: `ExchangeTokenUseCase`；infrastructure: `PrivyVerifier`（@privy-io/node v0.18）+ `JoseJwtService`（ES256 via jose v6）+ `PrismaUserRepository`；presentation: `POST /v1/auth/exchange`）。`authMiddleware` 支援 role hierarchy（user < reviewer < jury < admin）。env.ts 從 `JWT_SECRET`（HS256 placeholder）切換到 `JWT_PRIVATE_KEY_PEM` + `JWT_PUBLIC_KEY_PEM`（ES256 per rule 50）。新增 `PRIVY_APP_ID` / `PRIVY_APP_SECRET` / `PRIVY_VERIFICATION_KEY` / `DEFAULT_TENANT_ID`。
- [x] **Block 3: ReviewRegistry.sol** — 第一個 business contract。UUPS upgradeable（Initializable + AccessControlUpgradeable + PausableUpgradeable）。`submitReview(brokerId, contentHash, ipfsCid)` 存 tamper-proof anchor，full review 在 IPFS。無 deleteReview / editReview（不可篡改紅線）。Admin 只能 pause + upgrade。API-side SBT gate（per ADR-0019 D2）。48-slot `__gap`。17 tests 全綠（12 unit + 1 fuzz 1024 runs + 2 invariant 256 runs）。ADR-0019 紀錄設計決策。

- [x] `foundry.toml`：`solc_version = "0.8.24"` + `evm_version = "paris"`（OP Stack 通用，per ADR-0015 D3）+ `optimizer = true, optimizer_runs = 200` + `bytecode_hash = "none"` + `cbor_metadata = false`（BaseScan deterministic verify）+ `fuzz = { runs = 1024 }` + `invariant = { runs = 256, depth = 32 }` + `auto_detect_remappings = false` + `[fmt]` 完整規則（line 120、`uint256` long、double quote、thousands underscore、sorted imports、params-first multiline）

- [x] root `.prettierignore` 加 `lib/`（OZ 自己 `.prettierrc` 引用 `prettier-plugin-solidity`，會炸 `format:check`）
- [x] `packages/contracts/package.json` scripts 改實 forge / solhint commands（build、test、test:unit、test:ci `--no-match-test testFork`、fmt、fmt:check、lint 限 `test/**/*.sol` per D6、typecheck honest echo、clean delegates `forge clean`）

- [x] `packages/contracts/README.md` 完整 rewrite：Phase 0 toolchain ready 狀態、工具鏈表格（含 solc/forge/OZ/forge-std/solhint pinned versions）、目錄結構、first-time setup（`git submodule update --init --recursive` + `foundryup --install stable`）、critical contract rules、Phase 1+ 預告

#### 被投訴方答辯權階段化實現追蹤

被投訴方（券商）對投訴的「知情 + 答辯 + 公開回應」是 OpenTrade 公平精神的核心，但分散在三個 phase 完成。本段紀錄主軸視角，方便未來 agent 接手 M10 / Phase 3 時不會漏掉脈絡：

| 階段                      | 被投訴方能做什麼                                                      | 不能做什麼                        | 對應文件                                                                                                        |
| ------------------------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------- | --------------------------------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| Phase 1（M7，現在）       | 主動巡視自家公開頁面（`/brokers/:slug` 第三 tab）即可看到所有投訴     | 沒有通知 / 後台 / 答辯 / 公開回應 | 本 ADR-0029                                                                                                     |
| Phase 2.5（M10 商戶功能） | 商戶後台「我的被投訴」面板 + 通知 + 對每條投訴公開回應一次（C5 機制） | 沒有正式仲裁 / 陪審               | 待寫 [ADR-0033](./decisions/STAGING.md) S4（公開回應）+ [ADR-0037](./decisions/STAGING.md) S8（商戶可編輯範圍） |
| Phase 3（陪審團 V1）      | 7 天答辯窗口提交反駁 + 證據（質押）+ 陪審投票結果上鏈                 | —                                 | [ADR-0008](./decisions/0008-jury-phased-implementation.md)（已存在）                                            |

ADR-0029 D6 已預留 `respondsToReviewId` 欄位給 M10 公開回應使用（M7.1 純加 column 不 wire bidirectional relation，等 M10 商戶 broker response API 落地時再 wire 起來不會破壞本期 schema）。Phase 3 jury 答辯機制的資料形狀也已在 ADR-0029 D4 預留（`verifiedByUserId` 在 Phase 1 是 admin user id，Phase 3 改 nullable 並加 `verifiedByJuryProposalId`）。

**為什麼 Phase 1 不做商戶後台**：(a) 商戶 console 整體 self-service 生態屬於 M10 工作（per STAGING.md S8），現在加會違反 rule 96 commit 單一目的；(b) Phase 1 只有 30-50 種子用戶 + 100-200 邀請制散戶，量小到 admin 可人工聯繫商戶；(c) 投訴本身就上了公開頁面，rule 00 紅線（不刪、不隱藏）已經比 WikiFX 公平。

### 短期

- Dependabot PRs 批次 merge（15 個 pending）
- 評估 Next.js 14 → 15/16 升級
- 評估 Prisma 6 → 7 升級時機

## 待決策（懸而未決的問題）

### 2026-05-25 會議產生的 6 條衝突（C1-C6）

完整 context 見 [`docs/conversations/2026-05-25-team-meeting-strategy.md`](./conversations/2026-05-25-team-meeting-strategy.md) §「會議結論與既有設計衝突的 6 項」。User 已對 C1 拍板 remove，其餘 5 條進入 STAGING.md 排序。

- ⏳ **C1 — 五顆星 → 三向情緒**：User 已拍板 remove，由 M2 ADR-0028 + M3-M6 落地（會議自身有內部分歧 §02:42:10 — ADR 內 Alternatives Considered 段須列出五星論據再讓 user 終局確認）
- ❓ **C2 — Token Economy 引入時機**：與 [ADR-0007](./decisions/0007-no-token-in-v1.md) 衝突；會議 narrative 為 Pitch 用，code 落地待 Phase 5+（會 superseding ADR-0007）。STAGING.md 預留 ADR-0030
- ❓ **C3 — 智方便 (iAM Smart) L3 整合**：與 [ADR-0005](./decisions/0005-privy-aa-wallet.md) Privy 並存或取代；待 L3 jury 上線觸發。STAGING.md 預留 ADR-0031
- ❓ **C4 — HKMA Sandbox via HKSTP**：~HK$100k 入場費，與 [ADR-0002](./decisions/0002-aws-stack.md) 月費上限預算層級綁定；策略 + 預算決策。STAGING.md 預留 ADR-0032
- ❓ **C5 — 公開回應 (Broker Response) 機制**：商戶可對 review/complaint 公開回應一次；併入 M10 ADR-0037 商戶功能拍板
- ❓ **C6 — 內容過濾 + 標註不刪除**：需區分「鏈上 immutable」vs「indexer 可隱藏標註」兩層；M14 寫 ADR-0034 + 新 rule 52 content moderation

### 環境 / 帳號層級

- ✅ ~~**AWS 帳號**：是否已有？要建 dev/staging/prod 三帳號還是先一個？~~ → 已決定 per ADR-0016：兩 account（management `774126906499` + dev `371637912734`），day 1 用 Organizations，與 legacy AWS 帳號完全隔離
- ❓ **網域**：opentrade.io / .hk / .app — 之後再決定，不影響開發
- ❓ **AI 翻譯服務**：DeepL（主）vs OpenAI GPT（備）— 已預設 DeepL 主
- ❓ **GitHub Org 化**：目前是 `skyyuch/opentrade` 個人 repo。是否轉 GitHub Org `opentrade-hk`？
- ❓ **Repo Public/Private**：目前 GitHub 上是 Public（看 web 結果）。建議改 Private（在 SFC 高層董事正式加入前）。
- ❓ **Phase 4+ AWS region 增加 `us-east-1` opt-in**：CloudFront ACM SSL 證書 + Route 53 必須在 us-east-1（AWS 強制）。目前 management 與 dev account 都只 enable `ap-southeast-1`，待 Phase 4 上 prod 加 CloudFront 時再 opt-in（per ADR-0016 implementation notes）
- ❓ **Phase 4+ SCP 啟用**：region allow-list (`ap-southeast-1` + `us-east-1`)、`DenyRootUserActions`、`DenyMFADisable` 三條最低 SCP，Phase 4 prod 前必上線。需透過 `infra/terraform/modules/scp/`（per ADR-0016 D7 + rule 80 SCP 規範）
- ❓ **Phase 4+ `OpenTradeAdmin` permission set 拆分**：目前 single permission set，Phase 4+ 至少拆 `OpenTradeAdmin` / `OpenTradeReadOnly` / `OpenTradeBillingOnly`，當第二個人類加入或外部 auditor 接觸時觸發
- ❓ **Phase 4+ Identity Center 遷移到 corporate IdP**：目前用 Identity Center directory（內建）；當有公司 domain 與 Workspace / Okta 訂閱後考慮遷移（non-destructive，per ADR-0016 alternative G）
- ❓ **Phase 4+ 加 `opentrade-staging` + `opentrade-prod` sub-account**：當前只有 `opentrade-dev`；prod 上線前 staging / prod 各自獨立 account（per ADR-0002 + ADR-0016 D1）

### 業務層級

- ❓ **退休 SFC 高層董事人選**：何時正式加入？影響合規定位 narrative
- ❓ **預算上限**：本季 / 本年度的開發預算（影響 AWS 規模、設計師外包）
- ❓ **第一批種子陪審員邀請名單**：Phase 4 需要 30-50 位

### 技術層級

- ✅ ~~**多券商驗證策略**~~ → 已決策 per [ADR-0025](./decisions/0025-multi-broker-verification-strategy.md)，**Phase 1 實作 2026-05-24 完成**（6 個 commit：DB / API approve / API response / web /verify / console / review badge）。Phase 2 上鏈時機：當 (a) 有 user 被驗證 ≥ 3 家 broker，或 (b) KOL/jury 上鏈需要 broker mapping 時觸發。

- ❓ **License 選擇**：Business Source License 1.1 vs AGPL-3.0 — 上線前決定
- ❓ **設計師資源**：是否找 freelance 香港設計師（HK$30-80k 預算）做 Figma 高保真稿
- ❓ **KOL 訊號的 oracle**：Chainlink Price Feeds vs Pyth — Phase 2 開始前決定
- ❓ **Prisma 7 升級時機**：目前 pin 6.x（ADR-0013）；Prisma 7 driver-adapter 模式成熟後（>= 7.5+ 或 12 個月後）寫 successor ADR
- ❓ **User.email 加密策略**：Phase 0 `String?` 占位；Phase 1 auth flow 上線前需決定 envelope encryption（KMS）vs application-level encryption（AES-256-GCM）
- ✅ ~~**API 認證流程**：`JWT_SECRET` 目前是 placeholder~~ → 已實作 ES256 JWT（`JWT_PRIVATE_KEY_PEM` + `JWT_PUBLIC_KEY_PEM`）+ Privy token exchange `POST /v1/auth/exchange` + auth middleware with role hierarchy（Block 2c+2d）。`POST /v1/reviews` 已接入 authMiddleware('user')（Block 4）
- ❓ **`packages/db` 是否需要真實 build 步驟**：目前 `main: "./src/index.ts"`，dev 直消費 TS；ADR-0014 記錄為「延後」；何時觸發改建 = 多個 consumer 或 cold-start 變慢時
- ❓ **Next.js 14 → 15 / 16 升級評估**：commit number-six pin `~14.2.35`（per AGENTS.md tech table 寫定 Next 14）。但截至 2026-05 上游 latest 是 16.2.6，Next 15 也已 stable。升級會 touch：`params: Promise<{...}>` 改 sync 簽章、`middleware` 改名 `proxy`、Server Component caching 行為。寫 successor ADR 時機：完成 Phase 0 全部 commit 後集中處理
- ❓ **OZ v5 `ReentrancyGuard` 在 Upgradeable 合約的 storage 安全性**：v5 用 ERC-7201 namespaced storage，理論上 non-upgradeable `ReentrancyGuard` 可被 `UUPSUpgradeable` 合約直接 inherit。Phase 1 寫第一個業務合約（ReviewRegistry）時必須實測 storage layout（用 `forge inspect ReviewRegistry storage-layout`）並寫進 audit notes。若不安全則改用 `ReentrancyGuardTransient`（Cancun EVM 才能用，需先 ADR 切 `evm_version`）
- ❓ **Foundry version pin 策略**：本機 `foundryup --install stable` 抓到 `forge 1.7.1`。CI 透過 `foundry-toolchain` action 應 pin 同版本；何時 bump 寫 ADR：(a) 上游 1.8+ 帶來新 cheatcode 是 audit 必需；或 (b) v5 tag 解析 bug 修了之後（ADR-0015 D2 提到）
- ❓ **solhint 嚴格化時機**：ADR-0015 D5 約定 Phase 1 第一個業務合約 PR 時把 ruleset 從 warning-only 切 error-level，並 extend `solhint:recommended`。需在 Phase 1 同個 PR 內完成，避免「先 ship contract 再 tighten lint」的 backwards 流程

### 流程層級

- ❓ **Phase 2 開始前轉 PR-only flow**：目前 GitHub `main` 已設定 branch protection（必須走 PR + 必須通過 7 條 status checks），但 owner 帳號帶有 admin bypass 權限，Phase 1 大量 direct push 到 `main`（截至 2026-05-24 已累積 50+ commits 都是直推）。**Phase 2 開始前必須**：
  1. 列清楚 7 條 required status checks 的具體名稱（typecheck / lint / unit / build / forge / e2e / migration safety 之類），現在連名字都不確定
  2. 把它們在 `.github/workflows/` 補齊並讓 main 上每個 commit 都跑過至少一次（驗證沒漏跑）
  3. 寫一條新 ADR 紀錄：何時完全解除 admin bypass 權限（至少 jury / 第二位人類 contributor 加入時必須）
  4. 之後新功能一律走 `feature/xxx → PR → CI → squash merge`，違反 rule 70「不可 force push 到 main / 不可跳過 CI 直接 merge」的紅線

  目前 phase 1 開發節奏快、CI 還沒全綠，admin bypass 是務實之舉但不該長期化。觸發點：(a) 第二位人類 contributor 加入；(b) 完成 phase 1 / 進入 phase 2 之間；(c) 香港 SFC 高層董事正式加入並開始接觸 repo 之前 — 三者中最早的那個。

## 已知風險

| 風險                                                    | 嚴重度 | 緩解措施                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| ------------------------------------------------------- | ------ | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| 沒有 Web3 開發經驗                                      | 中     | 用 Foundry + OpenZeppelin + AI 輔助；上主網前必做第三方 audit                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| 冷啟動使用者來源                                        | 高     | 種子陪審員（業界人脈）+ Glassdoor 式 Give-to-Get 機制                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| 香港 SFC 第 4 類牌照風險                                | 中     | 純技術定位 + disclaimer + 退休 SFC 董事背書                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| KOL 不願意上鏈被監督                                    | 中     | 把不上鏈定位為紅旗，創造「上鏈 KOL」精英身分                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| AWS 成本失控                                            | 低     | dev 環境用最低規格，prod 規模隨用戶增長                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| ~~AI 翻譯品質不夠~~                                     | 已緩解 | ~~DeepL + 標明「機器翻譯」+ 後續引入人工校對~~ → ADR-0027 廢除自動翻譯，改 author-original + sourceLocale badge                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| ~~IPFS gateway HTTP `Content-Type` 無 `charset=utf-8`~~ | 已緩解 | ~~Pinata gateway cosmetic 問題；programmatic consumer 永遠 OK；瀏覽器 plain-view 看 UTF-8 中文會顯示 Latin-1 亂碼。修復需在 `apps/api` 加 `GET /v1/reviews/:id/ipfs-content` proxy endpoint~~ → 本 session M1.3 commit `16d7727` 完成；新 endpoint 強制 `Content-Type: application/json; charset=utf-8` + Web ReviewCard 加「IPFS 原文」link |
| 使用者 Mac 是全新 dev 環境                              | 已緩解 | 已透過 nvm 安裝 Node + pnpm；流程記錄在本檔                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| CI 完全無 AWS 認證，validate 抓不到 IAM/cost 回歸       | 中     | Phase 0 接受；rule 81 + ADR-0017 D11 + ADR-0018 D8 標明 Phase 4+ ADR-0019 加 OIDC + `terraform plan` PR comment 補上                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| Branch protection 為 UI 設定不可程式化                  | 低     | ADR-0018 D10 完整列表記住設定值；onboarding 第二位 contributor 時對表比設定                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |

## 環境基準（給新 session / 新人快速重建）

```bash
# Node 與 pnpm
node -v   # v22.22.3 (LTS Jod, 透過 nvm 管理)
pnpm -v   # 9.15.4 (透過 corepack 啟用)
docker --version  # 29.4.2 (Commit #4 起本機 dev DB 必備, per ADR-0012)
forge --version   # forge 1.7.1 (Commit number-eight 起本機合約開發必備, per ADR-0015)
aws --version     # aws-cli/2.x.x (Commit number-nine 起 AWS CLI 必備, per ADR-0016)

# 進入專案後
cd OpenTrade
cp .env.example .env                            # 首次：建立 gitignored .env
pnpm install                                    # 安裝全部依賴 (postinstall 跑 prisma generate)
docker compose up -d postgres                   # 起本機 Postgres 16
pnpm --filter @opentrade/db db:migrate:dev      # apply 任何 pending migration
pnpm --filter @opentrade/db db:seed             # 冪等 seed hk Tenant
pnpm typecheck                                  # 全包 type 檢查
pnpm lint                                       # 全包 ESLint
pnpm format:check                               # 全包 Prettier 檢查

# Commit number-five 起：起 API 並驗證
pnpm --filter @opentrade/api dev                # tsx watch http://localhost:4000
curl http://localhost:4000/v1/health            # 預期 200 OK + 真實 DB 延遲

# Commit number-six 起：起 web 並驗證跨包通訊
pnpm --filter @opentrade/web dev                # next dev http://localhost:3000
open http://localhost:3000/                     # zh-Hant 首頁（無 prefix per as-needed）
open http://localhost:3000/en/status            # 英文 /status 對接 /v1/health
open http://localhost:3000/zh-Hans/status       # 簡中

# Commit number-seven 起：起 console 並驗證 dark default + robots disallow
pnpm --filter @opentrade/console dev            # next dev http://localhost:3001
open http://localhost:3001/                     # zh-Hant 商戶後台（dark default + 4 張 card grid）
open http://localhost:3001/en                   # 英文 dashboard 殼
open http://localhost:3001/zh-Hans              # 簡中
curl http://localhost:3001/robots.txt           # → User-Agent: *  Disallow: /

# Commit number-eight 起：起 forge 工具鏈並驗證合約端到端
git submodule update --init --recursive         # 首次：拉 OZ + forge-std submodules
curl -L https://foundry.paradigm.xyz | bash     # 首次：安裝 foundryup
~/.foundry/bin/foundryup --install stable       # 首次：拉 forge 1.7.x binaries
forge --version                                  # → forge Version: 1.7.x
pnpm --filter @opentrade/contracts build        # forge build → 25 個 .sol 編譯成功
pnpm --filter @opentrade/contracts test         # forge test → 2 passed (Sanity)
pnpm --filter @opentrade/contracts lint         # solhint --noPrompt 'test/**/*.sol' → 0 warning
pnpm --filter @opentrade/contracts fmt:check    # forge fmt --check → exit 0

# Commit number-ten 起：CI 操作 + 驗證
gh --version                                     # → gh version 2.92.0 (本機從 release tarball 裝 ~/.local/bin/)
gh auth status                                   # 預期 Logged in 到 skyyuch + scopes 含 repo + workflow
gh pr create --base main --head <branch>         # 開 PR，自動套用 .github/pull_request_template.md
gh pr checks <pr-number>                         # watch CI check status（9 個 check：ci 4 + contracts 2 + terraform 3）
gh pr view <pr-number> --web                     # 開瀏覽器看 PR
# Terraform CI commands 本機驗證（與 .github/workflows/terraform.yml 跑的同義）
cd infra/terraform/bootstrap/state-backend
terraform init -backend=false -input=false       # 不碰 AWS，純 lock file resolve providers
terraform validate                                # → Success! The configuration is valid.
cd ../../environments/dev
terraform init -backend=false -input=false
terraform validate

# Bump AWS provider 等版本後重新 lock 三平台 hash（per rule 81 + ADR-0018）
terraform providers lock \
  -platform=linux_amd64 \
  -platform=darwin_arm64 \
  -platform=darwin_amd64
```

`.nvmrc` 已設為 `22`，使用者進到專案資料夾時 zsh hook 會自動切到正確 Node 版本。`~/.zshenv` 已被 `foundryup` 安裝器自動加 `export PATH="$PATH:$HOME/.foundry/bin"`，新開 terminal 直接可用 `forge`。

### AWS（Commit number-nine pre-flight 起，per ADR-0016 + rule 80）

```bash
# AWS Organization & Accounts
# Organization ID:        o-o5wm740m1h
# Management account:     skyyuch627      (774126906499)  ← 只放 Org / IDC / Billing
# Member account:         opentrade-dev   (371637912734)  ← Phase 0–3 全部開發資源

# IAM Identity Center
# Home region:            ap-southeast-1  (永久，不可改)
# Instance ID:            ssoins-82102c3fe7f6ab49
# Portal URL:             https://d-9667ab75a1.awsapps.com/start
# SSO user:               skyyu  (日常 email; root email 不日常用)
# Permission set:         OpenTradeAdmin  (AdministratorAccess + 8h session)

# Cost guardrails (in management account)
# - Budget phase-0-soft-cap   $50/month   80% actual + 100% forecast
# - Budget phase-0-hard-cap   $200/month  50% + 100% forecast
# - Cost Anomaly opentrade-anomaly-alerts  $25 OR 40%  daily summaries

# 本機首次設定
sudo installer -pkg ~/Downloads/AWSCLIV2.pkg -target /  # 裝 AWS CLI v2 官方 .pkg
aws --version                                            # 預期 aws-cli/2.x.x
aws sso login --profile opentrade-dev                    # 會跳瀏覽器點 Allow access
aws sts get-caller-identity --profile opentrade-dev      # 驗 Account=371637912734 + role=OpenTradeAdmin

# 日常使用
export AWS_PROFILE=opentrade-dev                         # 設進 ~/.zshrc 之後不用每次打 --profile
aws s3 ls                                                # 99% 操作走這個
aws ec2 describe-vpcs                                    # 都打到 dev sub-account

# 帳號 / Org 管理（極少數）
aws ... --profile opentrade-management

# Token 過期（每 8h）
aws sso login --profile opentrade-dev
```

`~/.aws/config` 含 `[default]`（legacy AWS 帳號保留）+ `[sso-session opentrade]` + `[profile opentrade-dev]` + `[profile opentrade-management]`。`~/.aws/credentials` 完全不動（legacy access key 留給舊項目）。SSO 與 access key 兩套 auth 互不打架；OpenTrade 永遠走 `--profile opentrade-dev`，legacy 走 `[default]`。

| 2026-05-24 | ADR-0025 Phase 1 implementation | Claude Opus 4.7 | 6 atomic commits implementing the multi-broker verified ledger. (1) `user_verified_brokers` table + relations on `User`/`Tenant`/`SbtVerificationRequest` + raw-SQL partial unique index `(userId, brokerSlug) WHERE status='APPROVED'` per ADR-0025 D2. (2) Approve flow rewritten as a single transaction: capture prev commitment → insert `UserVerifiedBroker` → emit `verification.broker_added` outbox event with hash-chain pointing to prev commitment (D5) → conditional tier promotion + `sbt.mint_requested` only when user is still L1 (D3, prevents AlreadyMinted on chain). `POST /verify-broker` rejects (CONFLICT) when (userId, brokerSlug) is already APPROVED. (3) `/verification-status` + `/admin/verifications` responses now ship `verifiedBrokers` arrays. (4) Web `/verify` adds 6th view `'adding'`; `BrokerCombobox.excludeSlugs` filters already-verified brokers from picker; `VerifyApprovedCard` lists verified brokers + "verify another broker" CTA. (5) Console case modal embeds `UserVerifiedBrokersPanel` highlighting current case among the user's full verified list. | 2026-05-24 | ADR-0025 post-rollout fixes — settings ledger drift + verify error i18n | Claude Opus 4.7 | 2 follow-up commits closing two regressions reported once verified-broker visibility shipped. (1) DB backfill — `20260524124500_backfill_user_verified_brokers` replays every APPROVED `sbt_verification_requests` row into `user_verified_brokers` using `verificationId` as the join key (idempotent via `ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING`). The user observed an L2-tier verified user seeing "you have not been verified for any broker yet" on `/settings` while `/verify` still rejected resubmissions for the same broker — a textbook ledger drift between the legacy table and the new ADR-0025 source-of-truth. The migration deliberately skips the `verification.broker_added` outbox emit (per ADR-0025 D5 those events are an audit trail for runtime approves, not a recovery hook; replaying them would spam stale notifications through the worker). Per ADR-0029 D7 Phase 1 doesn't put complaints on-chain so the handlers fall through to`processedAt`update without side effects; the file header docstring is updated to enumerate the three new event types and explicitly notes that`complaint.rejected`worker MUST NOT modify the Review row (rule 00「reject ≠ delete」 invariant — admin path already only mutates`adminNote`, but the doc puts the red line where the next worker maintainer reads first). **M7.3a** (`968fc0f`, 424 lines) `feat(api): bootstrap complaints domain types and Prisma repository`— atomic-but-large per the M5.1 / M6.0 / M6.2a precedent (three files type-circularly dependent — extracting them into separate commits leaves intermediate commits unable to compile). New`apps/api/src/domains/complaints/`directory with three files: (a)`domain/ComplaintEntity.ts`(116 lines) ships`SubmitComplaintInput`(required`evidenceIpfsCid`, optional `respondsToReviewId`, `kind: 'COMPLAINT'`literal carried through),`ComplaintRecord`(read-side projection mirroring`ReviewRecord`shape but with the complaint-specific fields surfaced), and a derived`ComplaintVerificationStatus = 'OPEN' | 'VERIFIED' | 'REJECTED'`— the public-facing status is **derived from`verifiedAt`+`adminNote`rather than persisted in a status column** per ADR-0029 D4 to keep`Review.status`(PENDING/CONFIRMED/FAILED) free for the on-chain pipeline that's reused for Phase 3 jury anchoring. (b)`domain/IComplaintRepository.ts`(82 lines) declares the port with`create`/`findById`/`list`/`applyVerification` — the verify/reject mutation parameter is a **discriminated union (`kind: 'verify' | 'reject'`) rather than two methods**, so the repository implementation can emit the correct outbox event in the same transaction and the rule-00 invariant ("verify branch never touches body / title / evidenceIpfsCid / contentHash / ipfsCid; reject branch only writes adminNote") is encoded into the type system rather than the docstring. (c) `infrastructure/PrismaComplaintRepository.ts`(229 lines) implements the port:`create`writes a`Review`row with`kind: 'COMPLAINT'`+ same-tx outbox`complaint.submitted`event (carries`complaintId`+`brokerSlug`+`userId`), `findById`includes a`kind = 'COMPLAINT'`guard so the repository never returns a review row by accident,`list`translates the derived`OPEN | VERIFIED | REJECTED | undefined`filter into the corresponding`verifiedAt IS NULL/NOT NULL`×`adminNote IS NULL/NOT NULL` boolean pair (`OPEN: verifiedAt IS NULL AND adminNote IS NULL`; `VERIFIED: verifiedAt IS NOT NULL`; `REJECTED: adminNote IS NOT NULL`; `undefined: no filter`), and `applyVerification`handles the two branches in a single transaction (verify: set`verifiedAt + verifiedByUserId`+ clear`adminNote`if previously rejected; reject: set`adminNote`+ clear`verifiedAt`if previously verified — never touches`deletedAt`/`body`/`title`/`evidenceIpfsCid`/`contentHash`/`ipfsCid`per rule 00). The file enforces a complaint must carry`rating: 1`to satisfy the still-NOT-NULL legacy`rating` column during the ADR-0028 D6 deprecation window (synthesized at the repository boundary not the API boundary so callers don't leak the legacy contract). **M7.3b** (`1d97dc0`, 332 lines) `feat(api): add complaint submit + list use cases and public endpoints`— five files: (a)`application/SubmitComplaintUseCase.ts`(71 lines) builds the IPFS payload with`kind: 'COMPLAINT'`discriminator +`evidenceIpfsCid`field on top of the v2 envelope established in M4.2 (so Phase 3 jury anchoring can reuse the same on-chain`submitReview`pipeline without migration), computes the keccak256`contentHash`deterministically (same hashing as reviews — Phase 3 jury verdict will anchor this hash on-chain), pins to IPFS via`PinataIpfsService`, then delegates to `complaintRepo.create`which atomically writes the row + outbox event. (b)`application/ListComplaintsUseCase.ts`(22 lines) is a thin wrapper around`complaintRepo.list`with explicit method-level docstring noting that the ADR-0029 D4 derived-status filter is the one place anyone should be translating`OPEN/VERIFIED/REJECTED`into DB conditions — clients further up the stack treat the three values as the canonical surface vocabulary. (c)`presentation/routes.ts`(229 lines) ships the public router:`POST /v1/complaints`requires`authMiddleware('reviewer')`(per ADR-0029 D3 only L2+ may file; rule 00 prevents anonymous accusations from contaminating the rule-00-immutable record) + zod body with required`evidenceIpfsCid`(string, IPFS CID shape) + required`brokerSlug`+ required`body`(10-2000 chars) + optional`title`(max 80 chars) + required`sentiment`(per ADR-0028 D4 — complaints carry sentiment so they participate in the broker-detail trust signal).`GET /v1/complaints/broker/:slug`is public-read with optional`?status=OPEN|VERIFIED|REJECTED`filter —`REJECTED`rows ship`adminNote`to the public view per ADR-0029 D4 so anyone can audit why the platform rejected the substantiation.`GET /v1/complaints/:id`is public-read single-fetch. (d)`index.ts`(8 lines) re-exports`complaintsRouter`. (e) `apps/api/src/http/server.ts`mounts`app.route('/v1/complaints', complaintsRouter)` between reviews and admin so existing routing topology stays clean. **M7.3c** (`f1f33cd`, 269 lines) `feat(api): add admin verify/reject endpoints with rule 00 invariant`— two files: (a)`application/VerifyComplaintUseCase.ts` (93 lines) **handles both verify and reject in a single class with a discriminated union input (`kind: 'verify' | 'reject'`)** rather than two parallel use cases — the read-side (load complaint by id + assert `kind === 'COMPLAINT'`+ assert exists) is 60% of the code and would inevitably drift across two separate use cases. The class loads the complaint, validates the action (verify is idempotent — re-verifying just refreshes the`verifiedByUserId`audit trail; admin can also reject a previously-verified complaint, which clears`verifiedAt`while setting`adminNote`so the audit history reflects the reversal), application-layer belt-suspenders re-validates`adminNote.length`is in`[5, 500]`for the reject branch (zod already does this at the route boundary, but defense-in-depth catches future internal callers that bypass the route schema), then delegates to`complaintRepo.applyVerification`which performs the mutation + emits`complaint.verified`or`complaint.rejected`outbox event in the same transaction. (b)`apps/api/src/domains/admin/presentation/routes.ts`adds`GET /admin/complaints`(with`brokerSlug`+ derived`status: 'OPEN'|'VERIFIED'|'REJECTED'|'ALL'`filter; the ALL bucket drops the status filter entirely for historical audit; broker name and author tier hydrated per cursor rule 51 + ADR-0026 three-language ship),`PATCH /admin/complaints/:id/verify`, and `PATCH /admin/complaints/:id/reject`(zod requires`adminNote: z.string().min(5).max(500, { message: '...' })`matching the ADR-0029 D4 mandate). All three endpoints sit under`authMiddleware('admin')`. The cross-domain admin path imports `VerifyComplaintUseCase`from the complaints domain so the URL space stays at the canonical`/v1/admin/complaints/...`per ADR-0029 D4 (vs the deferred-from option of`/v1/complaints/admin/...`which would be a route hierarchy violation with the existing`/v1/admin/users`/`/v1/admin/reviews`/`/v1/admin/verifications`admin URL pattern). The rule-00 invariant ("reject ≠ delete") is encoded in two testable places — the use case validates the discriminated union exhaustively, and the repository's`applyVerification` is the single SQL site that touches these columns. **M7.4** (`1112e9e`, 650 lines) `feat(console): add admin complaint moderation page per ADR-0029`— atomic-but-large per the VerificationsClient (787 lines) precedent: a single admin page with four tightly-coupled internal sub-components (StatusBadge / ComplaintRow / ComplaintDetailModal / RejectReasonModal) where lifting components to separate files would obscure the page's self-contained navigation logic. Seven files: (a)`apps/console/src/lib/api/client.ts`(60 lines insert) adds`fetchAdminComplaints(token, { brokerSlug, status, limit, offset, search })`+`verifyComplaint(token, id)`+`rejectComplaint(token, id, adminNote)`thin client wrappers, plus`AdminComplaintItem`and`AdminComplaintStatus = 'OPEN' | 'VERIFIED' | 'REJECTED'`types matching the API M7.3c shape. (b)`apps/console/src/app/[locale]/admin/complaints/page.tsx`(9 lines) is the route entry — renders`<ComplaintsClient />`. (c) `apps/console/src/app/[locale]/admin/complaints/ComplaintsClient.tsx`(541 lines) is the main client component: (i) StatusBadge differentiates OPEN (amber) / VERIFIED (red — VERIFIED-as-substantiated is a severity escalation in the platform context, not a green "all good" signal — chosen to match how merchant-side triage will read it) / REJECTED (muted slate); (ii) the page header has a 4-state filter (OPEN / VERIFIED / REJECTED / ALL — ALL drops`?status=`from the API call so historical audit is possible) and a search input that filters by broker slug, broker display name, or complaint body excerpt; (iii) ComplaintRow renders broker name (cursor rule 51 + ADR-0026 three-language`localizedBrokerName`helper), author wallet shortened, sentiment badge, body excerpt (clamp-2 lines), age-of-complaint, status badge, and a "View" CTA that opens ComplaintDetailModal; (iv) ComplaintDetailModal shows the full body + title + evidence IPFS link with`target="\_blank"`external link +`rel="noopener"`security pattern, the broker meta panel, the author meta panel (wallet + tier + role), and conditional action buttons — OPEN status shows red "Verify (substantiate)" CTA + grey "Reject" CTA; VERIFIED status shows the verifier admin id + verifiedAt timestamp + a single "Reject (overturn)" CTA that opens RejectReasonModal; REJECTED status shows the adminNote in a readonly callout (rule 00「reject ≠ delete」 — the public-facing reason stays visible) + a "Re-verify (overturn rejection)" CTA; (v) RejectReasonModal is a nested z-70 modal layered above the detail modal that requires a 5-500 char admin note matching the API zod constraint, with client-side validation feedback before submitting. (d)`apps/console/src/components/layout/AuthGate.tsx`adds`/admin/complaints`to the admin nav between Review management and Brokers + an`AlertTriangle`lucide icon. (e-g)`apps/console/messages/{zh-Hant,zh-Hans,en}.json`each gain 17 keys: nav.complaints + admin.complaintsTitle + admin.searchPlaceholder + 4 tab labels + 2 table column headers + admin.noComplaints empty state + 3 status badge labels + admin.complaintVerifyButton + 4 modal section titles + 1 reject button label. Reuses existing`rejectReasonTitle`and a few common labels from the`/admin/verifications`page to avoid duplication. **M7 verification points**: 7/9 commits done; lint-staged + prettier hooks pass on every commit;`pnpm --filter @opentrade/db typecheck`+`pnpm --filter @opentrade/api typecheck`+`pnpm --filter @opentrade/console typecheck`all green (the lone`apps/console`lint warning in`PrivyLoginButton`is pre-existing and unrelated to this session);`POST /v1/complaints`+`GET /v1/complaints/broker/:slug`+`GET /v1/complaints/:id`+`GET /v1/admin/complaints`+`PATCH /v1/admin/complaints/:id/verify`+`PATCH /v1/admin/complaints/:id/reject`six endpoints shipped through`apps/api/src/http/server.ts`; `/admin/complaints`browseable in console (waiting on M7.5 ComplaintForm before a full OPEN→VERIFIED + OPEN→REJECTED smoke test loop is possible). 14-milestone plan progress: still 7/14 milestones (M7 split into 9 sub-commits where 7 are now done) / 31/70 atomic commits. **Next pickup is M7.5**: extract`<EvidenceUpload>`primitive into`packages/ui`(PNG/JPEG/PDF + 5MB cap + Pinata pipeline reuse — the existing`/verify`page hand-rolled upload stays for now, primitive is initially scoped to ComplaintForm) +`apps/web` `ComplaintForm`client component (sentiment from M5`<SentimentPicker>`+ EvidenceUpload + body 10-2000 chars zod validation) + 3-language messages — estimated ~400 lines diff. **Design notes captured for future agents**: (a) M7.1`respondsToReviewId`is column-only without bidirectional Prisma relation — relation wiring waits for M10 broker-response API; this keeps the M7.1 schema commit single-purpose and avoids dragging an unrelated relation into a DB-only commit. (b)`adminNote String? @db.Text`is not in ADR-0029 D1's schema example but D4's reject flow demands it; reusing the`SbtVerificationRequest.adminNote`pattern means console + admin reviewers see the same shape twice in their workflow. (c) M7.3 was split into 3a/3b/3c rather than shipped as a single ~1000-line commit — 3a is unavoidably ~424 lines because the three domain files have circular type dependencies (entity ↔ port ↔ adapter), but 3b (332) + 3c (269) are independently deployable on top of 3a. (d) Admin endpoints live under`/v1/admin/complaints/...`per ADR-0029 D4 spec rather than nested under`/v1/complaints/admin/...`—`VerifyComplaintUseCase`is imported from the complaints domain into the admin domain's presentation layer, which is the established cross-domain pattern (admin domain owns`/v1/admin/users`+`/v1/admin/reviews`+`/v1/admin/verifications`already). (e) The verify/reject discriminated-union use case (single class, two branches) prevents a 60%-overlap drift between two parallel use cases — the read-side is the bulk of the code and the only branching is the mutation kind. (f)`ComplaintsClient.tsx`at 541 lines accepts the precedent of`VerificationsClient.tsx` (787 lines) — admin pages are inherently page-scoped and lifting sub-components like RejectReasonModal across files would lose the page's self-contained navigation invariants. **Rule 99 self-review**: this session's changes use only pre-existing patterns (DDD 4-layer with port + adapter, Prisma transaction emitting outbox event, discriminated-union mutation, lint-staged auto-fix on commit, cva for primitives — all well-trodden through M3-M6) — no new patterns introduced, no rule update required. **Handoff decision**: M7 upper half (7 commits) complete + context accumulated heavily (initial conversation summary already large + cross-`db`/`api`/`console`3-workspace 7-commit cycle) + domain about to switch (backend + admin → consumer-facing web UX + tests), per rule 98 conditions 1 + 2 the agent triggered handoff.
